9-32 DECKLISTS
==============



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on May 29, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_FrankKarsten.jpg)
By Frank Karsten











There is more to Grand Prix Manchester than just the Top 8. Below are the decklists of the players who finished in 9ththrough 32ndplace. Most of them were one match win and/or a tiebreaker boost away from the Top 8.







#### Petr Sochůrek's Bant Humans – 9th at Grand Prix Manchester 2016


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
